\subsection*{Typedefs}
\begin{Indent}{\bf Plugin interface}\par
{\em \label{_amgrpace149ed32fba50178284999ac0961ab}
A plugin interface that allows external runtime-\/loaded libraries to integrate with a client instance without modifications to the application code.

Plugins are loaded when referenced through the `plugin.library.paths` configuration property and operates on the {\ttfamily rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t} object prior {\ttfamily rd\_\-kafka\_\-t} instance creation.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
Plugins require the application to link librdkafka dynamically and not statically. Failure to do so will lead to missing symbols or finding symbols in another librdkafka library than the application was linked with. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
}\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
\item 
typedef \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a03509bab51072c72a8dcf52337e6d5cb}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}( \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a15f8730945790c3c5fb366f2970f73b8}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-plugin\_\-f\_\-conf\_\-init\_\-t} )(rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$conf, void $\ast$$\ast$plug\_\-opaquep, char $\ast$errstr, size\_\-t errstr\_\-size)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Plugin's configuration initializer method called each time the library is referenced from configuration (even if previously loaded by another client instance). \item\end{DoxyCompactList}\end{DoxyCompactItemize}
\end{Indent}

\begin{Indent}{\bf Queue API}\par
{\em \label{_amgrpd8cb6f5e9bac7d1d98d55db787f9bef3}
 Message queues allows the application to re-\/route consumed messages from multiple topic+partitions into one single queue point. This queue point containing messages from a number of topic+partitions may then be served by a single rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume$\ast$\_\-queue() call, rather than one call per topic+partition combination. }\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
\item

RD\_\-EXPORT const char $\ast$ \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_adece97d3cbdd6ca936df5b0663118c45}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-get\_\-debug\_\-contexts} (void)

\subsection*{Message headers}
\label{_amgrpf086fe31d049507e8e9ccf2adb6b3963}
Message headers consist of a list of (string key, binary value) pairs. Duplicate keys are supported and the order in which keys were added are retained.

Header values are considered binary and may have three types of value:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item proper value with size $>$ 0 and a valid pointer
\item empty value with size = 0 and any non-\/NULL pointer
\item null value with size = 0 and a NULL pointer
\end{DoxyItemize}

Headers require Apache Kafka broker version v0.11.0.0 or later.

Header operations are O(n). \begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
\item 
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_acaaff0aef7ee81e46ee7829412691ad7}{

\label{rdkafka_8h_acaaff0aef7ee81e46ee7829412691ad7}

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Create a new headers list. \item\end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\subsection*{Interceptors}
\label{_amgrp27990813574a6790e99690ca6c9443e6}
A callback interface that allows message interception for both producer and consumer data pipelines.

Except for the on\_\-new(), on\_\-conf\_\-set(), on\_\-conf\_\-dup() and on\_\-conf\_\-destroy() interceptors, interceptors are added to the newly created rd\_\-kafka\_\-t client instance. These interceptors MUST only be added from on\_\-new() and MUST NOT be added after \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a63d5cd86ab1f77772b2be170e1c09c24}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-new()} returns.

The on\_\-new(), on\_\-conf\_\-set(), on\_\-conf\_\-dup() and on\_\-conf\_\-destroy() interceptors are added to the configuration object which is later passed to \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a63d5cd86ab1f77772b2be170e1c09c24}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-new()} where on\_\-new() is called to allow addition of other interceptors.

Each interceptor reference consists of a display name (ic\_\-name), a callback function, and an application-\/specified opaque value that is passed as-\/is to the callback. The ic\_\-name must be unique for the interceptor implementation and is used to reject duplicate interceptor methods.

Any number of interceptors can be added and they are called in the order they were added, unless otherwise noted. The list of registered interceptor methods are referred to as interceptor chains.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Contrary to the Java client the librdkafka interceptor interface does not support message key and value modification. Message mutability is discouraged in the Java client and the combination of serializers and headers cover most use-\/cases.

Interceptors are NOT copied to the new configuration on \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8cbfe15c6978ff09870e82cb524c673d}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-dup()} since it would be hard for interceptors to track usage of the interceptor's opaque value. An interceptor should rely on the plugin, which will be copied in rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-conf\_\-dup(), to set up the initial interceptors. An interceptor should implement the on\_\-conf\_\-dup() method to manually set up its internal configuration on the newly created configuration object that is being copied-\/to based on the interceptor-\/specific configuration properties. conf\_\-dup() should thus be treated the same as conf\_\-init().

Interceptors are keyed by the interceptor type (on\_\-..()), the interceptor name (ic\_\-name) and the interceptor method function. Duplicates are not allowed and the ..\_\-add\_\-on\_\-..() method will return RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-CONFLICT if attempting to add a duplicate method. The only exception is on\_\-conf\_\-destroy() which may be added multiple times by the same interceptor to allow proper cleanup of interceptor configuration state. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyCompactItemize}
\item

typedef \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a03509bab51072c72a8dcf52337e6d5cb}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}( \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aca93ab41df25cab562b9a4cf6c0e7320}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-acknowledgement\_\-t} )(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, \hyperlink{structrd__kafka__message__t}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$rkmessage, void $\ast$ic\_\-opaque)
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em on\_\-acknowledgement() is called to inform interceptors that a message was succesfully delivered or permanently failed delivery. The interceptor chain is called from internal librdkafka background threads, or rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce$\ast$() if the partitioner failed. \item\end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em on\_\-commit() is called on completed or failed offset commit. It is called from internal librdkafka threads. \item\end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\subsection{Detailed Description}
Apache Kafka C/C++ consumer and producer client library. \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h}{rdkafka.h} contains the public API for librdkafka. The API is documented in this file as comments prefixing the function, type, enum, define, etc.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
For the C++ interface see \hyperlink{rdkafkacpp_8h}{rdkafkacpp.h}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}


\subsection{Define Documentation}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_aa2e242fb8620a32b650a40575bc7f98e}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-VERSION@{RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-VERSION}}
\index{RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-VERSION@{RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-VERSION}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-VERSION}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-VERSION~0x000b04c9}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_aa2e242fb8620a32b650a40575bc7f98e}


librdkafka version Interpreted as hex {\ttfamily MM.mm.rr.xx}:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item MM = Major
\item mm = minor
\item rr = revision
\item xx = pre-\/release id (0xff is the final release)
\end{DoxyItemize}

E.g.: {\ttfamily 0x000801ff} = 0.8.1

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This value should only be used during compile time, for runtime checks of version use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a83e363606ef2da2e91b7429b229dbc8e}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-version()} 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_aed25dba90c47adc8ae51d098dca2aed9}{

\subsubsection[{RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-DEBUG\_\-CONTEXTS}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}\#define RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-DEBUG\_\-CONTEXTS~\char`\"{}all,generic,broker,topic,metadata,feature,queue,msg,protocol,cgrp,security,fetch,interceptor,plugin,consumer\char`\"{}}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_aed25dba90c47adc8ae51d098dca2aed9}


Supported debug contexts. (compile time). \begin{Desc}
\item[\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000001}{Deprecated}]This compile time value may be outdated at runtime due to linking another version of the library. Use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_adece97d3cbdd6ca936df5b0663118c45}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-get\_\-debug\_\-contexts()} instead. \end{Desc}

                (const char *)NAME, (const void *)VALUE, (ssize_t)LEN
\end{DoxyCode}

\subsection{Typedef Documentation}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a15f8730945790c3c5fb366f2970f73b8}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-plugin\_\-f\_\-conf\_\-init\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-plugin\_\-f\_\-conf\_\-init\_\-t}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-plugin\_\-f\_\-conf\_\-init\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-plugin\_\-f\_\-conf\_\-init\_\-t}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-plugin\_\-f\_\-conf\_\-init\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}( {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-plugin\_\-f\_\-conf\_\-init\_\-t})(rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$conf, void $\ast$$\ast$plug\_\-opaquep, char $\ast$errstr, size\_\-t errstr\_\-size)}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a15f8730945790c3c5fb366f2970f73b8}


Plugin's configuration initializer method called each time the library is referenced from configuration (even if previously loaded by another client instance). \begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This method MUST be implemented by plugins and have the symbol name {\ttfamily conf\_\-init} 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em conf}]Configuration set up to this point. \item[{\em plug\_\-opaquep}]Plugin can set this pointer to a per-\/configuration opaque pointer. \item[{\em errstr}]String buffer of size {\ttfamily errstr\_\-size} where plugin must write a human readable error string in the case the initializer fails (returns non-\/zero).\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
A plugin may add an on\_\-conf\_\-destroy() interceptor to clean up plugin-\/specific resources created in the plugin's conf\_\-init() method.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR on success or an error code on error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_adb146aa9dbc3a5d4bb4a5b53c1b86b0d}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-t}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-t}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-res\_\-t}( {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-t})(rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$conf, const char $\ast$name, const char $\ast$val, char $\ast$errstr, size\_\-t errstr\_\-size, void $\ast$ic\_\-opaque)}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_adb146aa9dbc3a5d4bb4a5b53c1b86b0d}


on\_\-conf\_\-set() is called from rd\_\-kafka\_\-$\ast$\_\-conf\_\-set() in the order the interceptors were added. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em ic\_\-opaque}]The interceptor's opaque pointer specified in ..add..(). \item[{\em name}]The configuration property to set. \item[{\em val}]The configuration value to set, or NULL for reverting to default in which case the previous value should be freed. \item[{\em errstr}]A human readable error string in case the interceptor fails. \item[{\em errstr\_\-size}]Maximum space (including ) in {\ttfamily errstr}.\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-CONF\_\-RES\_\-OK if the property was known and successfully handled by the interceptor, RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-CONF\_\-RES\_\-INVALID if the property was handled by the interceptor but the value was invalid, or RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-CONF\_\-RES\_\-UNKNOWN if the interceptor did not handle this property, in which case the property is passed on on the interceptor in the chain, finally ending up at the built-\/in configuration handler. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a4339f06d7d4d02d06fbc401d279daeb2}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-dup\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-dup\_\-t}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-dup\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-dup\_\-t}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-dup\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}( {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-dup\_\-t})(rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$new\_\-conf, const rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$old\_\-conf, size\_\-t filter\_\-cnt, const char $\ast$$\ast$filter, void $\ast$ic\_\-opaque)}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a4339f06d7d4d02d06fbc401d279daeb2}


on\_\-conf\_\-dup() is called from \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8cbfe15c6978ff09870e82cb524c673d}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-dup()} in the order the interceptors were added and is used to let an interceptor re-\/register its conf interecptors with a new opaque value. The on\_\-conf\_\-dup() method is called prior to the configuration from {\ttfamily old\_\-conf} being copied to {\ttfamily new\_\-conf}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em ic\_\-opaque}]The interceptor's opaque pointer specified in ..add..().\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR on success or an error code on failure (which is logged but otherwise ignored).
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
No on\_\-conf\_\-$\ast$ interceptors are copied to the new configuration object on \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8cbfe15c6978ff09870e82cb524c673d}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-dup()}. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-destroy\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-destroy\_\-t}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}

\label{rdkafka_8h_a39c5416d05a8262ae0a2937853c99257}


on\_\-conf\_\-destroy() is called from rd\_\-kafka\_\-$\ast$\_\-conf\_\-destroy() in the order the interceptors were added. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}

\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a045854635d67e89de3098a0d5f53cc39}{

\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-new\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}( {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-new\_\-t})(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, const rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$conf, void $\ast$ic\_\-opaque, char $\ast$errstr, size\_\-t errstr\_\-size)}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a045854635d67e89de3098a0d5f53cc39}


on\_\-new() is called from \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a63d5cd86ab1f77772b2be170e1c09c24}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-new()} prior toreturning the newly created client instance to the application. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em rk}]The client instance. \item[{\em conf}]The client instance's final configuration. \item[{\em ic\_\-opaque}]The interceptor's opaque pointer specified in ..add..(). \item[{\em errstr}]A human readable error string in case the interceptor fails. \item[{\em errstr\_\-size}]Maximum space (including ) in {\ttfamily errstr}.\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an error code on failure, the error is logged but otherwise ignored.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The {\ttfamily rk} client instance will not be fully set up when this interceptor is called and the interceptor MUST NOT call any other rk-\/specific APIs than rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-add..(). 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a3eae9c1d37ab4effd55bb8ed5177ac4d}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-destroy\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-destroy\_\-t}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-destroy\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-destroy\_\-t}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-destroy\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}( {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-destroy\_\-t})(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, void $\ast$ic\_\-opaque)}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a3eae9c1d37ab4effd55bb8ed5177ac4d}


on\_\-destroy() is called from \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ac052e92621dcaa3a336dbf826e0d7794}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-destroy()} or (\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a63d5cd86ab1f77772b2be170e1c09c24}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-new()} if \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a63d5cd86ab1f77772b2be170e1c09c24}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-new()} fails during initialization). 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em rk}]The client instance. \item[{\em ic\_\-opaque}]The interceptor's opaque pointer specified in ..add..(). \end{DoxyParams}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a4b71a63f37c4d94cdb1d05e88f120988}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-send\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-send\_\-t}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-send\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-send\_\-t}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-send\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}( {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-send\_\-t})(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$rkmessage, void $\ast$ic\_\-opaque)}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a4b71a63f37c4d94cdb1d05e88f120988}


on\_\-send() is called from rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce$\ast$() (et.al) prior to the partitioner being called. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em rk}]The client instance. \item[{\em rkmessage}]The message being produced. Immutable. \item[{\em ic\_\-opaque}]The interceptor's opaque pointer specified in ..add..().\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This interceptor is only used by producer instances.

The {\ttfamily rkmessage} object is NOT mutable and MUST NOT be modified by the interceptor.

If the partitioner fails or an unknown partition was specified, the on\_\-acknowledgement() interceptor chain will be called from within the rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce$\ast$() call to maintain send-\/acknowledgement symmetry.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an error code on failure, the error is logged but otherwise ignored. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_aca93ab41df25cab562b9a4cf6c0e7320}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-acknowledgement\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-acknowledgement\_\-t}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-acknowledgement\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-acknowledgement\_\-t}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-acknowledgement\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}( {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-acknowledgement\_\-t})(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$rkmessage, void $\ast$ic\_\-opaque)}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_aca93ab41df25cab562b9a4cf6c0e7320}


on\_\-acknowledgement() is called to inform interceptors that a message was succesfully delivered or permanently failed delivery. The interceptor chain is called from internal librdkafka background threads, or rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce$\ast$() if the partitioner failed. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em rk}]The client instance. \item[{\em rkmessage}]The message being produced. Immutable. \item[{\em ic\_\-opaque}]The interceptor's opaque pointer specified in ..add..().\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This interceptor is only used by producer instances.

The {\ttfamily rkmessage} object is NOT mutable and MUST NOT be modified by the interceptor.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The on\_\-acknowledgement() method may be called from internal librdkafka threads. An on\_\-acknowledgement() interceptor MUST NOT call any librdkafka API's associated with the {\ttfamily rk}, or perform any blocking or prolonged work.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an error code on failure, the error is logged but otherwise ignored. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_aeafe5c26d64281c1f9a2e2f77f774fa4}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-consume\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-consume\_\-t}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-consume\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-consume\_\-t}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-consume\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}( {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-consume\_\-t})(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$rkmessage, void $\ast$ic\_\-opaque)}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_aeafe5c26d64281c1f9a2e2f77f774fa4}


on\_\-consume() is called just prior to passing the message to the application in \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a65cc6cb9bd72c4084f074af0361ceddf}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-poll()}, rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume$\ast$(), the event interface, etc. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em rk}]The client instance. \item[{\em rkmessage}]The message being consumed. Immutable. \item[{\em ic\_\-opaque}]The interceptor's opaque pointer specified in ..add..().\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This interceptor is only used by consumer instances.

The {\ttfamily rkmessage} object is NOT mutable and MUST NOT be modified by the interceptor.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an error code on failure, the error is logged but otherwise ignored. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a4ce7c3dfd327ce6512245302be4fe067}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-commit\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-commit\_\-t}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-commit\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-commit\_\-t}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-commit\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}( {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-commit\_\-t})(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, const {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$offsets, {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} err, void $\ast$ic\_\-opaque)}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a4ce7c3dfd327ce6512245302be4fe067}


on\_\-commit() is called on completed or failed offset commit. It is called from internal librdkafka threads. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em rk}]The client instance. \item[{\em offsets}]List of topic+partition+offset+error that were committed. The error message of each partition should be checked for error. \item[{\em ic\_\-opaque}]The interceptor's opaque pointer specified in ..add..().\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This interceptor is only used by consumer instances.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The on\_\-commit() interceptor is called from internal librdkafka threads. An on\_\-commit() interceptor MUST NOT call any librdkafka API's associated with the {\ttfamily rk}, or perform any blocking or prolonged work.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an error code on failure, the error is logged but otherwise ignored. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_afae0abf1b1a5a85da0e3e22c78e3c5bf}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-request\_\-sent\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-request\_\-sent\_\-t}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-request\_\-sent\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-request\_\-sent\_\-t}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-request\_\-sent\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}typedef {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}( {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-request\_\-sent\_\-t})(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, int sockfd, const char $\ast$brokername, int32\_\-t brokerid, int16\_\-t ApiKey, int16\_\-t ApiVersion, int32\_\-t CorrId, size\_\-t size, void $\ast$ic\_\-opaque)}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_afae0abf1b1a5a85da0e3e22c78e3c5bf}


on\_\-request\_\-sent() is called when a request has been fully written to a broker TCP connections socket. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em rk}]The client instance. \item[{\em sockfd}]Socket file descriptor. \item[{\em brokername}]Broker request is being sent to. \item[{\em brokerid}]Broker request is being sent to. \item[{\em ApiKey}]Kafka protocol request type. \item[{\em ApiVersion}]Kafka protocol request type version. \item[{\em Corrid}]Kafka protocol request correlation id. \item[{\em size}]Size of request. \item[{\em ic\_\-opaque}]The interceptor's opaque pointer specified in ..add..().\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
The on\_\-request\_\-sent() interceptor is called from internal librdkafka broker threads. An on\_\-request\_\-sent() interceptor MUST NOT call any librdkafka API's associated with the {\ttfamily rk}, or perform any blocking or prolonged work.
\end{DoxyWarning}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
an error code on failure, the error is logged but otherwise ignored. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a03509bab51072c72a8dcf52337e6d5cb}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}enum {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t}}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a03509bab51072c72a8dcf52337e6d5cb}


Error codes. The negative error codes delimited by two underscores ({\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-}..) denotes errors internal to librdkafka and are displayed as {\ttfamily $\backslash$\char`\"{}Local: $<$error string..$>$$\backslash$\char`\"{}}, while the error codes delimited by a single underscore ({\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-}..) denote broker errors and are displayed as {\ttfamily $\backslash$\char`\"{}Broker: $<$error string..$>$$\backslash$\char`\"{}}.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ab7bfc925e8d63851511b88a1cee94d6d}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-err2str()} to translate an error code a human readable string 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}

\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ae7b90c323d460e0276d79f6ab69e93b7}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-last\_\-error@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-last\_\-error}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-last\_\-error@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-last\_\-error}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-last\_\-error}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-last\_\-error (void)}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ae7b90c323d460e0276d79f6ab69e93b7}


Returns the last error code generated by a legacy API call in the current thread. The legacy APIs are the ones using errno to propagate error value, namely:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ab1dcba74a35e8f3bfe3270ff600581d8}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-new()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_acf07475e5e85e63fc5321a1087288cd4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-stop()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a53511739a2cf498b8d88287fef6873ce}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a303fa0f0da7f3c28bed35570adc983c6}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8ff0b80fccb3a5bd31b1baaf20e4ca16}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-queue()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae24d8ebf1ea15ed8ea0ea40f74662736}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce()}
\end{DoxyItemize}

The main use for this function is to avoid converting system {\ttfamily errno} values to rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t codes for legacy APIs.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The last error is stored per-\/thread, if multiple rd\_\-kafka\_\-t handles are used in the same application thread the developer needs to make sure \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae7b90c323d460e0276d79f6ab69e93b7}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-last\_\-error()} is called immediately after a failed API call.

errno propagation from librdkafka is not safe on Windows and should not be used, use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae7b90c323d460e0276d79f6ab69e93b7}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-last\_\-error()} instead. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_abeabf8589c657d7a3ec5a1411a7de91d}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno2err@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno2err}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno2err@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno2err}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno2err}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT RD\_\-DEPRECATED {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno2err (int {\em errnox})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_abeabf8589c657d7a3ec5a1411a7de91d}


Converts the system errno value {\ttfamily errnox} to a rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t error code upon failure from the following functions:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ab1dcba74a35e8f3bfe3270ff600581d8}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-new()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_acf07475e5e85e63fc5321a1087288cd4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-stop()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a53511739a2cf498b8d88287fef6873ce}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a303fa0f0da7f3c28bed35570adc983c6}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8ff0b80fccb3a5bd31b1baaf20e4ca16}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-queue()}
\item \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae24d8ebf1ea15ed8ea0ea40f74662736}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce()}. 
\end{DoxyItemize}
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em errnox}]System errno value to convert\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Appropriate error code for {\ttfamily errnox} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
A better alternative is to call \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae7b90c323d460e0276d79f6ab69e93b7}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-last\_\-error()} immediately after any of the above functions return -\/1 or NULL.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{Desc}
\item[\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000002}{Deprecated}]Use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae7b90c323d460e0276d79f6ab69e93b7}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-last\_\-error()} to retrieve the last error code set by the legacy librdkafka APIs.\end{Desc}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae7b90c323d460e0276d79f6ab69e93b7}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-last\_\-error()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a8aa1b1a41d2fc0c487f519663609df4f}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT RD\_\-DEPRECATED int rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno (void)}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a8aa1b1a41d2fc0c487f519663609df4f}


Returns the thread-\/local system errno. On most platforms this is the same as {\ttfamily errno} but in case of different runtimes between library and application (e.g., Windows static DLLs) this provides a means for exposing the errno librdkafka uses.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The value is local to the current calling thread.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{Desc}
\item[\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000003}{Deprecated}]Use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae7b90c323d460e0276d79f6ab69e93b7}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-last\_\-error()} to retrieve the last error code set by the legacy librdkafka APIs. \end{Desc}

\label{rdkafka_8h_ad86e25f9787e647588fc2067705de10e}


Add header with name {\ttfamily name} and value {\ttfamily val} (copied) of size {\ttfamily size} (not including null-\/terminator). 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em name}]Header name. \item[{\em name\_\-size}]Header name size (not including the null-\/terminator). If -\/1 the {\ttfamily name} length is automatically acquired using strlen(). \item[{\em value}]Pointer to header value, or NULL (set size to 0 or -\/1). \item[{\em value\_\-size}]Size of header value. If -\/1 the {\ttfamily value} is assumed to be a null-\/terminated string and the length is automatically acquired using strlen().\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-READ\_\-ONLY if the headers are read-\/only, else RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR.

Find last header in list {\ttfamily hdrs} matching {\ttfamily name}. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em name}]Header to find (last match). \item[{\em valuep}](out) Set to a (null-\/terminated) const pointer to the value (may be NULL). \item[{\em sizep}](out) Set to the value's size (not including null-\/terminator).\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR if an entry was found, else RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-NOENT.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The returned pointer in {\ttfamily valuep} includes a trailing null-\/terminator that is not accounted for in {\ttfamily sizep}. 

The returned pointer is only valid as long as the headers list and the header item is valid. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

Returns the message timestamp for a consumed message. The timestamp is the number of milliseconds since the epoch (UTC).

{\ttfamily tstype} (if not NULL) is updated to indicate the type of timestamp.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-headers}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-headers (const {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em rkmessage}, \/  rd\_\-kafka\_\-headers\_\-t $\ast$$\ast$ {\em hdrsp})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_aaccd9ee7e1c73b89d86ed41db3b86e68}


Get the message header list. The returned pointer in {\ttfamily $\ast$hdrsp} is associated with the {\ttfamily rkmessage} and must not be used after destruction of the message object or the header list is replaced with \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a99e46233e57fc4f5783d8ae374584bbe}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-set\_\-headers()}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR if headers were returned, RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-NOENT if the message has no headers, or another error code if the headers could not be parsed.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Headers require broker version 0.11.0.0 or later.

As an optimization the raw protocol headers are parsed on the first call to this function. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_af89ef912d3c1ff66ea612fda27c0a643}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-detach\_\-headers@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-detach\_\-headers}}

\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-detach\_\-headers}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-detach\_\-headers ({\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em rkmessage}, \/  rd\_\-kafka\_\-headers\_\-t $\ast$$\ast$ {\em hdrsp})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_af89ef912d3c1ff66ea612fda27c0a643}


Get the message header list and detach the list from the message making the application the owner of the headers. The application must eventually destroy the headers using \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa31d7a8707a729839e54422ca976d8b1}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-headers\_\-destroy()}. The message's headers will be set to NULL. Otherwise same semantics as \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aaccd9ee7e1c73b89d86ed41db3b86e68}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-headers()}

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aaccd9ee7e1c73b89d86ed41db3b86e68}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-headers} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a99e46233e57fc4f5783d8ae374584bbe}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-set\_\-headers@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-set\_\-headers}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-set\_\-headers@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-set\_\-headers}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-set\_\-headers}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-set\_\-headers ({\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em rkmessage}, \/  rd\_\-kafka\_\-headers\_\-t $\ast$ {\em hdrs})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a99e46233e57fc4f5783d8ae374584bbe}


Replace the message's current headers with a new list. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em hdrs}]New header list. The message object assumes ownership of the list, the list will be destroyed automatically with the message object. The new headers list may be updated until the message object is passed or returned to librdkafka.\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The existing headers object, if any, will be destroyed. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-new}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t$\ast$ rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-new (void)}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_aa7459bd22e8cfa81aa8c2480a4a0304c}


Create configuration object. When providing your own configuration to the {\ttfamily rd\_\-kafka\_\-$\ast$\_\-new\_\-$\ast$}() calls the rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t objects needs to be created with this function which will set up the defaults. I.e.: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
   rd_kafka_conf_t *myconf;
   rd_kafka_conf_res_t res;

   myconf = rd_kafka_conf_new();
   res = rd_kafka_conf_set(myconf, "socket.timeout.ms", "600",
                           errstr, sizeof(errstr));
   if (res != RD_KAFKA_CONF_OK)
      die("%s\n", errstr);
   
   rk = rd_kafka_new(..., myconf);
\end{DoxyCode}


Please see CONFIGURATION.md for the default settings or use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa52f3a5a08207e14386739fe336e57be}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-properties\_\-show()} to provide the information at runtime.

The properties are identical to the Apache Kafka configuration properties whenever possible.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A new rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t object with defaults set.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_abb1b319278333e8cdee9442da7f135e8}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set()}, \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_af3669dacf78c5c0eb536d65cb45d0491}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-destroy()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a8cbfe15c6978ff09870e82cb524c673d}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-dup@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-dup}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-dup@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-dup}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-dup}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t$\ast$ rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-dup (const rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a8cbfe15c6978ff09870e82cb524c673d}


Creates a copy/duplicate of configuration object {\ttfamily conf}. \begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Interceptors are NOT copied to the new configuration object. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-conf\_\-dup 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_abb1b319278333e8cdee9442da7f135e8}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-res\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  const char $\ast$ {\em name}, \/  const char $\ast$ {\em value}, \/  char $\ast$ {\em errstr}, \/  size\_\-t {\em errstr\_\-size})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_abb1b319278333e8cdee9442da7f135e8}


Sets a configuration property. {\ttfamily conf} must have been previously created with \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa7459bd22e8cfa81aa8c2480a4a0304c}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-new()}.

Fallthrough: Topic-\/level configuration properties may be set using this interface in which case they are applied on the {\ttfamily default\_\-topic\_\-conf}. If no {\ttfamily default\_\-topic\_\-conf} has been set one will be created. Any sub-\/sequent \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a138aa4881c8703dd6b69f22ddc454f63}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-default\_\-topic\_\-conf()} calls will replace the current default topic configuration.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-res\_\-t} to indicate success or failure. In case of failure {\ttfamily errstr} is updated to contain a human readable error string. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a075b15c4141784fdc271de217005a41f}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-dr\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-dr\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-dr\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-dr\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-dr\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-dr\_\-cb (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  void($\ast$)(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, void $\ast$payload, size\_\-t len, {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} err, void $\ast$opaque, void $\ast$msg\_\-opaque) {\em dr\_\-cb})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a075b15c4141784fdc271de217005a41f}
\begin{Desc}
\item[\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000004}{Deprecated}]See \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ac1c9946aee26e10de2661fcf2242ea8a}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-dr\_\-msg\_\-cb()} \end{Desc}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ac1c9946aee26e10de2661fcf2242ea8a}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-dr\_\-msg\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-dr\_\-msg\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-dr\_\-msg\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-dr\_\-msg\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-dr\_\-msg\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-dr\_\-msg\_\-cb (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  void($\ast$)(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, const {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$rkmessage, void $\ast$opaque) {\em dr\_\-msg\_\-cb})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ac1c9946aee26e10de2661fcf2242ea8a}


{\bfseries Producer:} Set delivery report callback in provided {\ttfamily conf} object. The delivery report callback will be called once for each message accepted by \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae24d8ebf1ea15ed8ea0ea40f74662736}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce()} (et.al) with {\ttfamily err} set to indicate the result of the produce request.

The callback is called when a message is succesfully produced or if librdkafka encountered a permanent failure, or the retry counter for temporary errors has been exhausted.

An application must call \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll()} at regular intervals to serve queued delivery report callbacks. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a10db731dc1a295bd9884e4f8cb199311}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-rebalance\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-rebalance\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-rebalance\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-rebalance\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-rebalance\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-rebalance\_\-cb (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  void($\ast$)(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} err, {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$partitions, void $\ast$opaque) {\em rebalance\_\-cb})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a10db731dc1a295bd9884e4f8cb199311}


{\bfseries Consumer:} Set rebalance callback for use with coordinated consumer group balancing. The {\ttfamily err} field is set to either RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-ASSIGN\_\-PARTITIONS or RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-REVOKE\_\-PARTITIONS and 'partitions' contains the full partition set that was either assigned or revoked.

Registering a {\ttfamily rebalance\_\-cb} turns off librdkafka's automatic partition assignment/revocation and instead delegates that responsibility to the application's {\ttfamily rebalance\_\-cb}.

The rebalance callback is responsible for updating librdkafka's assignment set based on the two events: RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-ASSIGN\_\-PARTITIONS and RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-REVOKE\_\-PARTITIONS but should also be able to handle arbitrary rebalancing failures where {\ttfamily err} is neither of those. \begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
In this latter case (arbitrary error), the application must call rd\_\-kafka\_\-assign(rk, NULL) to synchronize state.
\end{DoxyRemark}
Without a rebalance callback this is done automatically by librdkafka but registering a rebalance callback gives the application flexibility in performing other operations along with the assinging/revocation, such as fetching offsets from an alternate location (on assign) or manually committing offsets (on revoke).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The {\ttfamily partitions} list is destroyed by librdkafka on return return from the rebalance\_\-cb and must not be freed or saved by the application.
\end{DoxyRemark}
The following example shows the application's responsibilities: 
\begin{DoxyCode}
    static void rebalance_cb (rd_kafka_t *rk, rd_kafka_resp_err_t err,
                              rd_kafka_topic_partition_list_t *partitions,
                              void *opaque) {

        switch (err)
        {
          case RD_KAFKA_RESP_ERR__ASSIGN_PARTITIONS:
             // application may load offets from arbitrary external
             // storage here and update \p partitions

             rd_kafka_assign(rk, partitions);
             break;

          case RD_KAFKA_RESP_ERR__REVOKE_PARTITIONS:
             if (manual_commits) // Optional explicit manual commit
                 rd_kafka_commit(rk, partitions, 0); // sync commit

             rd_kafka_assign(rk, NULL);
             break;

          default:
             handle_unlikely_error(err);
             rd_kafka_assign(rk, NULL); // sync state
             break;
         }
    }
\end{DoxyCode}
 \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a1ab8bb9e8d8cdd5906f9e060b506f2eb}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-offset\_\-commit\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-offset\_\-commit\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-offset\_\-commit\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-offset\_\-commit\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-offset\_\-commit\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-offset\_\-commit\_\-cb (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  void($\ast$)(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} err, {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$offsets, void $\ast$opaque) {\em offset\_\-commit\_\-cb})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a1ab8bb9e8d8cdd5906f9e060b506f2eb}


{\bfseries Consumer:} Set offset commit callback for use with consumer groups. The results of automatic or manual offset commits will be scheduled for this callback and is served by \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a65cc6cb9bd72c4084f074af0361ceddf}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-poll()}.

If no partitions had valid offsets to commit this callback will be called with {\ttfamily err} == RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-NO\_\-OFFSET which is not to be considered an error.

The {\ttfamily offsets} list contains per-\/partition information:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily offset:} committed offset (attempted)
\item {\ttfamily err:} commit error 
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ace721ef3b7c22d0c111ec747ef039a90}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-error\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-error\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-error\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-error\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-error\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-error\_\-cb (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  void($\ast$)(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, int err, const char $\ast$reason, void $\ast$opaque) {\em error\_\-cb})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ace721ef3b7c22d0c111ec747ef039a90}


Set error callback in provided conf object. The error callback is used by librdkafka to signal critical errors back to the application.

If no {\ttfamily error\_\-cb} is registered then the errors will be logged instead. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a04160826ad039d42c10edec456163fa7}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-throttle\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-throttle\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-throttle\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-throttle\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-throttle\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-throttle\_\-cb (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  void($\ast$)(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, const char $\ast$broker\_\-name, int32\_\-t broker\_\-id, int throttle\_\-time\_\-ms, void $\ast$opaque) {\em throttle\_\-cb})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a04160826ad039d42c10edec456163fa7}


Set throttle callback. The throttle callback is used to forward broker throttle times to the application for Produce and Fetch (consume) requests.

Callbacks are triggered whenever a non-\/zero throttle time is returned by the broker, or when the throttle time drops back to zero.

An application must call \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll()} or \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a65cc6cb9bd72c4084f074af0361ceddf}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-poll()} at regular intervals to serve queued callbacks.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Requires broker version 0.9.0 or later. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a06ade2ca41f32eb82c6f7e3d4acbe19f}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-log\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-log\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-log\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-log\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-log\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-log\_\-cb (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  void($\ast$)(const rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, int level, const char $\ast$fac, const char $\ast$buf) {\em log\_\-cb})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a06ade2ca41f32eb82c6f7e3d4acbe19f}


Set logger callback. The default is to print to stderr, but a syslog logger is also available, see rd\_\-kafka\_\-log\_\-print and rd\_\-kafka\_\-log\_\-syslog for the builtin alternatives. Alternatively the application may provide its own logger callback. Or pass {\ttfamily func} as NULL to disable logging.

This is the configuration alternative to the deprecated \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a9e4af9adee414af74c7817403f7c4a53}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-logger()}

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The log\_\-cb will be called spontaneously from librdkafka's internal threads unless logs have been forwarded to a poll queue through {\ttfamily \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a5c8a3be2f797560b2a39bf56dbd7622d}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-log\_\-queue()}}. An application MUST NOT call any librdkafka APIs or do any prolonged work in a non-\/forwarded {\ttfamily log\_\-cb}. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a597d00432e3ca22174d18e7e348fb766}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-stats\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-stats\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-stats\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-stats\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-stats\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-stats\_\-cb (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  int($\ast$)(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, char $\ast$json, size\_\-t json\_\-len, void $\ast$opaque) {\em stats\_\-cb})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a597d00432e3ca22174d18e7e348fb766}


Set statistics callback in provided conf object. The statistics callback is triggered from \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll()} every {\ttfamily statistics.interval.ms} (needs to be configured separately). Function arguments:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily rk} -\/ Kafka handle
\item {\ttfamily json} -\/ String containing the statistics data in JSON format
\item {\ttfamily json\_\-len} -\/ Length of {\ttfamily json} string.
\item {\ttfamily opaque} -\/ Application-\/provided opaque.
\end{DoxyItemize}

If the application wishes to hold on to the {\ttfamily json} pointer and free it at a later time it must return 1 from the {\ttfamily stats\_\-cb}. If the application returns 0 from the {\ttfamily stats\_\-cb} then librdkafka will immediately free the {\ttfamily json} pointer. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a0467a6c20d5af69a29a63b530962ecbf}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-socket\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-socket\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-socket\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-socket\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-socket\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-socket\_\-cb (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  int($\ast$)(int domain, int type, int protocol, void $\ast$opaque) {\em socket\_\-cb})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a0467a6c20d5af69a29a63b530962ecbf}


Set socket callback. The socket callback is responsible for opening a socket according to the supplied {\ttfamily domain}, {\ttfamily type} and {\ttfamily protocol}. The socket shall be created with {\ttfamily CLOEXEC} set in a racefree fashion, if possible.

Default:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item on linux: racefree CLOEXEC
\item others : non-\/racefree CLOEXEC
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The callback will be called from an internal librdkafka thread. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a53dd1b77019324170d0168617fdaf040}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-connect\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-connect\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-connect\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-connect\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-connect\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-connect\_\-cb (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  int($\ast$)(int sockfd, const struct sockaddr $\ast$addr, int addrlen, const char $\ast$id, void $\ast$opaque) {\em connect\_\-cb})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a53dd1b77019324170d0168617fdaf040}


Set connect callback. The connect callback is responsible for connecting socket {\ttfamily sockfd} to peer address {\ttfamily addr}. The {\ttfamily id} field contains the broker identifier.

{\ttfamily connect\_\-cb} shall return 0 on success (socket connected) or an error number (errno) on error.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The callback will be called from an internal librdkafka thread. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ab55c7ddc46a354e3f57b5b209e5ec3c7}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-closesocket\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-closesocket\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-closesocket\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-closesocket\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-closesocket\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-closesocket\_\-cb (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  int($\ast$)(int sockfd, void $\ast$opaque) {\em closesocket\_\-cb})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ab55c7ddc46a354e3f57b5b209e5ec3c7}


Set close socket callback. Close a socket (optionally opened with socket\_\-cb()).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The callback will be called from an internal librdkafka thread. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a467bb7b1ac070fee536227d6ae9cc551}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-open\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-open\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-open\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-open\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-open\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-open\_\-cb (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  int($\ast$)(const char $\ast$pathname, int flags, mode\_\-t mode, void $\ast$opaque) {\em open\_\-cb})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a467bb7b1ac070fee536227d6ae9cc551}


Set open callback. The open callback is responsible for opening the file specified by pathname, flags and mode. The file shall be opened with {\ttfamily CLOEXEC} set in a racefree fashion, if possible.

Default:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item on linux: racefree CLOEXEC
\item others : non-\/racefree CLOEXEC
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The callback will be called from an internal librdkafka thread. 
\end{DoxyRemark}

Sets the default topic configuration to use for automatically subscribed topics (e.g., through pattern-\/matched topics). The topic config object is not usable after this call. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_abe9f0f77e9145eb1a62c3258ac495b97}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-get@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-get}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-get@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-get}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-get}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-res\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-get (const rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  const char $\ast$ {\em name}, \/  char $\ast$ {\em dest}, \/  size\_\-t $\ast$ {\em dest\_\-size})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_abe9f0f77e9145eb1a62c3258ac495b97}


Retrieve configuration value for property {\ttfamily name}. If {\ttfamily dest} is non-\/NULL the value will be written to {\ttfamily dest} with at most {\ttfamily dest\_\-size}.

{\ttfamily $\ast$dest\_\-size} is updated to the full length of the value, thus if {\ttfamily $\ast$dest\_\-size} initially is smaller than the full length the application may reallocate {\ttfamily dest} to fit the returned {\ttfamily $\ast$dest\_\-size} and try again.

If {\ttfamily dest} is NULL only the full length of the value is returned.

Fallthrough: Topic-\/level configuration properties from the {\ttfamily default\_\-topic\_\-conf} may be retrieved using this interface.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-CONF\_\-OK} if the property name matched, else {\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-CONF\_\-UNKNOWN}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-partitioner\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-partitioner\_\-cb}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-partitioner\_\-cb@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-partitioner\_\-cb}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-partitioner\_\-cb}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-partitioner\_\-cb (rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em topic\_\-conf}, \/  int32\_\-t($\ast$)(const rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t $\ast$rkt, const void $\ast$keydata, size\_\-t keylen, int32\_\-t partition\_\-cnt, void $\ast$rkt\_\-opaque, void $\ast$msg\_\-opaque) {\em partitioner})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_abfc790b5e36c56ea6d79fdc32c57becf}


{\bfseries Producer:} Set partitioner callback in provided topic conf object. The partitioner may be called in any thread at any time, it may be called multiple times for the same message/key.

Partitioner function constraints:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item MUST NOT call any rd\_\-kafka\_\-$\ast$() functions except: \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad24c6cc7f37271e292f8105c64d77758}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-available()}
\item MUST NOT block or execute for prolonged periods of time.
\item MUST return a value between 0 and partition\_\-cnt-\/1, or the special {\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-PARTITION\_\-UA} value if partitioning could not be performed. 
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a760cee234c441d32f9421874a74e06d4}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-msg\_\-order\_\-cmp@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-msg\_\-order\_\-cmp}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-msg\_\-order\_\-cmp@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-msg\_\-order\_\-cmp}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-msg\_\-order\_\-cmp}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-msg\_\-order\_\-cmp (rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em topic\_\-conf}, \/  int($\ast$)(const {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$a, const {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$b) {\em msg\_\-order\_\-cmp})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a760cee234c441d32f9421874a74e06d4}


{\bfseries Producer:} Set message queueing order comparator callback. The callback may be called in any thread at any time, it may be called multiple times for the same message.

Ordering comparator function constraints:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item MUST be stable sort (same input gives same output).
\item MUST NOT call any rd\_\-kafka\_\-$\ast$() functions.
\item MUST NOT block or execute for prolonged periods of time.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The comparator shall compare the two messages and return:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item $<$ 0 if message {\ttfamily a} should be inserted before message {\ttfamily b}.
\item $>$=0 if message {\ttfamily a} should be inserted after message {\ttfamily b}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Insert sorting will be used to enqueue the message in the correct queue position, this comes at a cost of O(n).

If `queuing.strategy=fifo` new messages are enqueued to the tail of the queue regardless of msg\_\-order\_\-cmp, but retried messages are still affected by msg\_\-order\_\-cmp.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyWarning}{Warning}
THIS IS AN EXPERIMENTAL API, SUBJECT TO CHANGE OR REMOVAL, DO NOT USE IN PRODUCTION. 
\end{DoxyWarning}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ad24c6cc7f37271e292f8105c64d77758}{

\label{rdkafka_8h_ad24c6cc7f37271e292f8105c64d77758}


Check if partition is available (has a leader broker). \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
