\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a63d5cd86ab1f77772b2be170e1c09c24}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-new@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-new}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-new@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-new}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-new}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT rd\_\-kafka\_\-t$\ast$ rd\_\-kafka\_\-new ({\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-type\_\-t} {\em type}, \/  rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  char $\ast$ {\em errstr}, \/  size\_\-t {\em errstr\_\-size})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a63d5cd86ab1f77772b2be170e1c09c24}


Creates a new Kafka handle and starts its operation according to the specified {\ttfamily type} ({\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-CONSUMER} or {\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-PRODUCER}). {\ttfamily conf} is an optional struct created with `rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-new()` that will be used instead of the default configuration. The {\ttfamily conf} object is freed by this function on success and must not be used or destroyed by the application sub-\/sequently. See `rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set()` et.al for more information.

{\ttfamily errstr} must be a pointer to memory of at least size {\ttfamily errstr\_\-size} where `rd\_\-kafka\_\-new()` may write a human readable error message in case the creation of a new handle fails. In which case the function returns NULL.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
{\bfseries RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-CONSUMER:} When a new {\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-CONSUMER} rd\_\-kafka\_\-t handle is created it may either operate in the legacy simple consumer mode using the \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start()} interface, or the High-\/level KafkaConsumer API. 

An application must only use one of these groups of APIs on a given rd\_\-kafka\_\-t RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-CONSUMER handle.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
The Kafka handle on success or NULL on error (see {\ttfamily errstr})
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
To destroy the Kafka handle, use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ac052e92621dcaa3a336dbf826e0d7794}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-destroy()}. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ac052e92621dcaa3a336dbf826e0d7794}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-destroy@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-destroy}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-destroy@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-destroy}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-destroy}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-destroy (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ac052e92621dcaa3a336dbf826e0d7794}


Destroy Kafka handle. \begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This is a blocking operation. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a856d7ecba1aa64e5c89ac92b445cdda6}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-memberid@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-memberid}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-memberid@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-memberid}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-memberid}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT char$\ast$ rd\_\-kafka\_\-memberid (const rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a856d7ecba1aa64e5c89ac92b445cdda6}


Returns this client's broker-\/assigned group member id. \begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This currently requires the high-\/level KafkaConsumer
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An allocated string containing the current broker-\/assigned group member id, or NULL if not available. The application must free the string with {\ttfamily free()} or \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a50178b3d3266c9eeb0b5981377833572}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-mem\_\-free()} 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a261ba8c649756fbc7fbcd442ae481a18}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-clusterid@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-clusterid}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-clusterid@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-clusterid}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-clusterid}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT char$\ast$ rd\_\-kafka\_\-clusterid (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a261ba8c649756fbc7fbcd442ae481a18}


Returns the ClusterId as reported in broker metadata. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em timeout\_\-ms}]If there is no cached value from metadata retrieval then this specifies the maximum amount of time (in milliseconds) the call will block waiting for metadata to be retrieved. Use 0 for non-\/blocking calls.\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Requires broker version $>$=0.10.0 and api.version.request=true.

The application must free the returned pointer using \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a50178b3d3266c9eeb0b5981377833572}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-mem\_\-free()}.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a newly allocated string containing the ClusterId, or NULL if no ClusterId could be retrieved in the allotted timespan. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ab1dcba74a35e8f3bfe3270ff600581d8}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-new@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-new}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-new@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-new}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-new}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t$\ast$ rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-new (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  const char $\ast$ {\em topic}, \/  rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ab1dcba74a35e8f3bfe3270ff600581d8}


Creates a new topic handle for topic named {\ttfamily topic}. {\ttfamily conf} is an optional configuration for the topic created with `rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-new()` that will be used instead of the default topic configuration. The {\ttfamily conf} object is freed by this function and must not be used or destroyed by the application sub-\/sequently. See `rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-conf\_\-set()` et.al for more information.

Topic handles are refcounted internally and calling \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ab1dcba74a35e8f3bfe3270ff600581d8}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-new()} again with the same topic name will return the previous topic handle without updating the original handle's configuration. Applications must eventually call \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a91f46cd29d4f9abacd3ee3633c01d8ff}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-destroy()} for each succesfull call to \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ab1dcba74a35e8f3bfe3270ff600581d8}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-new()} to clear up resources.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the new topic handle or NULL on error (use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_abeabf8589c657d7a3ec5a1411a7de91d}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno2err()} to convert system {\ttfamily errno} to an rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t error code.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a91f46cd29d4f9abacd3ee3633c01d8ff}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-destroy()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a91f46cd29d4f9abacd3ee3633c01d8ff}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-destroy@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-destroy}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-destroy@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-destroy}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-destroy}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-destroy (rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkt})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a91f46cd29d4f9abacd3ee3633c01d8ff}


Loose application's topic handle refcount as previously created with `rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-new()`. \begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Since topic objects are refcounted (both internally and for the app) the topic object might not actually be destroyed by this call, but the application must consider the object destroyed. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT int rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}


Polls the provided kafka handle for events. Events will cause application provided callbacks to be called.

The {\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms} argument specifies the maximum amount of time (in milliseconds) that the call will block waiting for events. For non-\/blocking calls, provide 0 as {\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms}. To wait indefinately for an event, provide -\/1.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
An application should make sure to call poll() at regular intervals to serve any queued callbacks waiting to be called.
\end{DoxyRemark}
Events:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item delivery report callbacks (if dr\_\-cb/dr\_\-msg\_\-cb is configured) \mbox{[}producer\mbox{]}
\item error callbacks (\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ace721ef3b7c22d0c111ec747ef039a90}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-error\_\-cb()}) \mbox{[}all\mbox{]}
\item stats callbacks (\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a597d00432e3ca22174d18e7e348fb766}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-stats\_\-cb()}) \mbox{[}all\mbox{]}
\item throttle callbacks (\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a04160826ad039d42c10edec456163fa7}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-throttle\_\-cb()}) \mbox{[}all\mbox{]}
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of events served. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a111628df6c84716c4b550f8509ac6a6d}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-yield@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-yield}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-yield@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-yield}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-yield}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-yield (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a111628df6c84716c4b550f8509ac6a6d}


Cancels the current callback dispatcher (\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll()}, \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a303fa0f0da7f3c28bed35570adc983c6}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback()}, etc). A callback may use this to force an immediate return to the calling code (caller of e.g. \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll()}) without processing any further events.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This function MUST ONLY be called from within a librdkafka callback. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a293cb2aac290c157702d3b82f5c14fce}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-pause\_\-partitions@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-pause\_\-partitions}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-pause\_\-partitions@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-pause\_\-partitions}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-pause\_\-partitions}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-pause\_\-partitions (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em partitions})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a293cb2aac290c157702d3b82f5c14fce}


Pause producing or consumption for the provided list of partitions. Success or error is returned per-\/partition {\ttfamily err} in the {\ttfamily partitions} list.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ad05819f26887a916ad2047d96a7b4bf2}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-resume\_\-partitions@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-resume\_\-partitions}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-resume\_\-partitions@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-resume\_\-partitions}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-resume\_\-partitions}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-resume\_\-partitions (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em partitions})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ad05819f26887a916ad2047d96a7b4bf2}


Resume producing consumption for the provided list of partitions. Success or error is returned per-\/partition {\ttfamily err} in the {\ttfamily partitions} list.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a4550ff7d014f08406666124573f70495}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-query\_\-watermark\_\-offsets@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-query\_\-watermark\_\-offsets}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-query\_\-watermark\_\-offsets@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-query\_\-watermark\_\-offsets}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-query\_\-watermark\_\-offsets}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-query\_\-watermark\_\-offsets (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  const char $\ast$ {\em topic}, \/  int32\_\-t {\em partition}, \/  int64\_\-t $\ast$ {\em low}, \/  int64\_\-t $\ast$ {\em high}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a4550ff7d014f08406666124573f70495}


Query broker for low (oldest/beginning) and high (newest/end) offsets for partition. Offsets are returned in {\ttfamily $\ast$low} and {\ttfamily $\ast$high} respectively.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR on success or an error code on failure. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ad1d338cebde98a76050e61301f631d82}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-get\_\-watermark\_\-offsets@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-get\_\-watermark\_\-offsets}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-get\_\-watermark\_\-offsets@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-get\_\-watermark\_\-offsets}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-get\_\-watermark\_\-offsets}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-get\_\-watermark\_\-offsets (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  const char $\ast$ {\em topic}, \/  int32\_\-t {\em partition}, \/  int64\_\-t $\ast$ {\em low}, \/  int64\_\-t $\ast$ {\em high})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ad1d338cebde98a76050e61301f631d82}


Get last known low (oldest/beginning) and high (newest/end) offsets for partition. The low offset is updated periodically (if statistics.interval.ms is set) while the high offset is updated on each fetched message set from the broker.

If there is no cached offset (either low or high, or both) then RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-OFFSET\_\-INVALID will be returned for the respective offset.

Offsets are returned in {\ttfamily $\ast$low} and {\ttfamily $\ast$high} respectively.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR on success or an error code on failure.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Shall only be used with an active consumer instance. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ae308aaf534807cfd4c71e423fc214929}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-offsets\_\-for\_\-times@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-offsets\_\-for\_\-times}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-offsets\_\-for\_\-times@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-offsets\_\-for\_\-times}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-offsets\_\-for\_\-times}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-offsets\_\-for\_\-times (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em offsets}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ae308aaf534807cfd4c71e423fc214929}


Look up the offsets for the given partitions by timestamp. The returned offset for each partition is the earliest offset whose timestamp is greater than or equal to the given timestamp in the corresponding partition.

The timestamps to query are represented as {\ttfamily offset} in {\ttfamily offsets} on input, and {\ttfamily offset} will contain the offset on output.

The function will block for at most {\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms} milliseconds.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Duplicate Topic+Partitions are not supported. 

Per-\/partition errors may be returned in {\ttfamily \hyperlink{structrd__kafka__topic__partition__t_ab9370931853903657d7cabc9643d336e}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-t.err}} 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR if offsets were be queried (do note that per-\/partition errors might be set), RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-TIMED\_\-OUT if not all offsets could be fetched within {\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms}, RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-INVALID\_\-ARG if the {\ttfamily offsets} list is empty, RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-UNKNOWN\_\-PARTITION if all partitions are unknown, RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-LEADER\_\-NOT\_\-AVAILABLE if unable to query leaders for the given partitions. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a50178b3d3266c9eeb0b5981377833572}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-mem\_\-free@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-mem\_\-free}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-mem\_\-free@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-mem\_\-free}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-mem\_\-free}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-mem\_\-free (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  void $\ast$ {\em ptr})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a50178b3d3266c9eeb0b5981377833572}


Free pointer returned by librdkafka. This is typically an abstraction for the free(3) call and makes sure the application can use the same memory allocator as librdkafka for freeing pointers returned by librdkafka.

In standard setups it is usually not necessary to use this interface rather than the free(3) functione.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a50178b3d3266c9eeb0b5981377833572}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-mem\_\-free()} must only be used for pointers returned by APIs that explicitly mention using this function for freeing. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a2b59178eb7e88d40510a89f3f2d98b44}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-new@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-new}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-new@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-new}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-new}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t$\ast$ rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-new (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a2b59178eb7e88d40510a89f3f2d98b44}


Create a new message queue. See \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8e952d7961169471f69c7ddc87041258}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start\_\-queue()}, \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8ff0b80fccb3a5bd31b1baaf20e4ca16}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-queue()}, et.al. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a9421b3d450f1489cf46f68d49c5ea61e}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-destroy@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-destroy}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-destroy@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-destroy}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-destroy}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-destroy (rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkqu})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a9421b3d450f1489cf46f68d49c5ea61e}
Destroy a queue, purging all of its enqueued messages. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a7f3d675ee029a52bf85fb28f83c38863}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-main@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-main}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-main@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-main}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-main}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t$\ast$ rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-main (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a7f3d675ee029a52bf85fb28f83c38863}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a reference to the main librdkafka event queue. This is the queue served by \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll()}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a9421b3d450f1489cf46f68d49c5ea61e}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-destroy()} to loose the reference. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_acacdb55ae7cb6abfbde89621e512b078}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-consumer@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-consumer}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-consumer@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-consumer}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-consumer}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t$\ast$ rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-consumer (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_acacdb55ae7cb6abfbde89621e512b078}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a reference to the librdkafka consumer queue. This is the queue served by \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a65cc6cb9bd72c4084f074af0361ceddf}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-poll()}.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a9421b3d450f1489cf46f68d49c5ea61e}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-destroy()} to loose the reference.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a9421b3d450f1489cf46f68d49c5ea61e}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-destroy()} MUST be called on this queue prior to calling \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a37b54d329e12d745889defe96e7d043d}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-close()}. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ad5319a26efb9f843c6029f7dd54b742d}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-partition@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-partition}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-partition@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-partition}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-partition}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t$\ast$ rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-get\_\-partition (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  const char $\ast$ {\em topic}, \/  int32\_\-t {\em partition})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ad5319a26efb9f843c6029f7dd54b742d}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a reference to the partition's queue, or NULL if partition is invalid.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a9421b3d450f1489cf46f68d49c5ea61e}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-destroy()} to loose the reference.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a9421b3d450f1489cf46f68d49c5ea61e}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-destroy()} MUST be called on this queue

This function only works on consumers. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a5e2e5571d14636d289f963a270b8e338}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-forward@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-forward}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-forward@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-forward}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-forward}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-forward (rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t $\ast$ {\em src}, \/  rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t $\ast$ {\em dst})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a5e2e5571d14636d289f963a270b8e338}


Forward/re-\/route queue {\ttfamily src} to {\ttfamily dst}. If {\ttfamily dst} is {\ttfamily NULL} the forwarding is removed. The internal refcounts for both queues are increased.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Regardless of whether {\ttfamily dst} is NULL or not, after calling this function, {\ttfamily src} will not forward it's fetch queue to the consumer queue. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a5c8a3be2f797560b2a39bf56dbd7622d}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-log\_\-queue@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-log\_\-queue}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-log\_\-queue@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-log\_\-queue}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-log\_\-queue}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-log\_\-queue (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkqu})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a5c8a3be2f797560b2a39bf56dbd7622d}


Forward librdkafka logs (and debug) to the specified queue for serving with one of the ..poll() calls. This allows an application to serve log callbacks ({\ttfamily log\_\-cb}) in its thread of choice.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em rkqu}]Queue to forward logs to. If the value is NULL the logs are forwarded to the main queue.\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The configuration property {\ttfamily log.queue} MUST also be set to true.

librdkafka maintains its own reference to the provided queue.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR on success or an error code on error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a8f24368f4ff0e042907773f532f62e57}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-length@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-length}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-length@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-length}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-length}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT size\_\-t rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-length (rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkqu})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a8f24368f4ff0e042907773f532f62e57}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the current number of elements in queue. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_acbdd13ab480f6320b2842981eebce784}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-io\_\-event\_\-enable@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-io\_\-event\_\-enable}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-io\_\-event\_\-enable@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-io\_\-event\_\-enable}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-io\_\-event\_\-enable}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-io\_\-event\_\-enable (rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkqu}, \/  int {\em fd}, \/  const void $\ast$ {\em payload}, \/  size\_\-t {\em size})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_acbdd13ab480f6320b2842981eebce784}


Enable IO event triggering for queue. To ease integration with IO based polling loops this API allows an application to create a separate file-\/descriptor that librdkafka will write {\ttfamily payload} (of size {\ttfamily size}) to whenever a new element is enqueued on a previously empty queue.

To remove event triggering call with {\ttfamily fd} = -\/1.

librdkafka will maintain a copy of the {\ttfamily payload}.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
When using forwarded queues the IO event must only be enabled on the final forwarded-\/to (destination) queue. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT int rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start (rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkt}, \/  int32\_\-t {\em partition}, \/  int64\_\-t {\em offset})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}


Start consuming messages for topic {\ttfamily rkt} and {\ttfamily partition} at offset {\ttfamily offset} which may either be an absolute {\ttfamily }(0..N) or one of the logical offsets:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-OFFSET\_\-BEGINNING
\item RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-OFFSET\_\-END
\item RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-OFFSET\_\-STORED
\item RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-OFFSET\_\-TAIL. 
\end{DoxyItemize}rdkafka will attempt to keep {\ttfamily queued.min.messages} (config property) messages in the local queue by repeatedly fetching batches of messages from the broker until the threshold is reached.

The application shall use one of the `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume$\ast$()` functions to consume messages from the local queue, each kafka message being represented as a `rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t $\ast$` object.

`rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start()` must not be called multiple times for the same topic and partition without stopping consumption first with `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-stop()`.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success or -\/1 on error in which case errno is set accordingly:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item EBUSY -\/ Conflicts with an existing or previous subscription (RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-CONFLICT)
\item EINVAL -\/ Invalid offset, or incomplete configuration (lacking group.id) (RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-INVALID\_\-ARG)
\item ESRCH -\/ requested {\ttfamily partition} is invalid. (RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-UNKNOWN\_\-PARTITION)
\item ENOENT -\/ topic is unknown in the Kafka cluster. (RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-UNKNOWN\_\-TOPIC)
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
Use `rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno2err()` to convert sytem {\ttfamily errno} to `rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t` \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a8e952d7961169471f69c7ddc87041258}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start\_\-queue@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start\_\-queue}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start\_\-queue@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start\_\-queue}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start\_\-queue}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT int rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start\_\-queue (rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkt}, \/  int32\_\-t {\em partition}, \/  int64\_\-t {\em offset}, \/  rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkqu})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a8e952d7961169471f69c7ddc87041258}


Same as \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae21dcd2d8c6195baf7f9f4952d7e12d4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start()} but re-\/routes incoming messages to the provided queue {\ttfamily rkqu} (which must have been previously allocated with `rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-new()`. The application must use one of the `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-$\ast$\_\-queue()` functions to receive fetched messages.

`rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start\_\-queue()` must not be called multiple times for the same topic and partition without stopping consumption first with `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-stop()`. `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start()` and `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start\_\-queue()` must not be combined for the same topic and partition. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_acf07475e5e85e63fc5321a1087288cd4}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-stop@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-stop}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-stop@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-stop}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-stop}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT int rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-stop (rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkt}, \/  int32\_\-t {\em partition})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_acf07475e5e85e63fc5321a1087288cd4}


Stop consuming messages for topic {\ttfamily rkt} and {\ttfamily partition}, purging all messages currently in the local queue. NOTE: To enforce synchronisation this call will block until the internal fetcher has terminated and offsets are committed to configured storage method.

The application needs to be stop all consumers before calling `rd\_\-kafka\_\-destroy()` on the main object handle.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success or -\/1 on error (see `errno`). 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a6667b162931982e9827e3d86ad22ec7d}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-seek@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-seek}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-seek@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-seek}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-seek}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-seek (rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkt}, \/  int32\_\-t {\em partition}, \/  int64\_\-t {\em offset}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a6667b162931982e9827e3d86ad22ec7d}


Seek consumer for topic+partition to {\ttfamily offset} which is either an absolute or logical offset. If {\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms} is not 0 the call will wait this long for the seek to be performed. If the timeout is reached the internal state will be unknown and this function returns `RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-TIMED\_\-OUT`. If {\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms} is 0 it will initiate the seek but return immediately without any error reporting (e.g., async).

This call triggers a fetch queue barrier flush.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
`RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-NO\_\-ERROR` on success else an error code. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t}$\ast$ rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume (rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkt}, \/  int32\_\-t {\em partition}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}


Consume a single message from topic {\ttfamily rkt} and {\ttfamily partition}. {\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms} is maximum amount of time to wait for a message to be received. Consumer must have been previously started with `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start()`.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a message object on success or {\ttfamily NULL} on error. The message object must be destroyed with `rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-destroy()` when the application is done with it.
\end{DoxyReturn}
Errors (when returning NULL):
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ETIMEDOUT -\/ {\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms} was reached with no new messages fetched.
\item ENOENT -\/ {\ttfamily rkt} + {\ttfamily partition} is unknown. (no prior `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-start()` call)
\end{DoxyItemize}

NOTE: The returned message's {\ttfamily }..-\/$>$err must be checked for errors. NOTE: {\ttfamily }..-\/$>$err {\ttfamily ==} {\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-PARTITION\_\-EOF} signals that the end of the partition has been reached, which should typically not be considered an error. The application should handle this case (e.g., ignore).

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
on\_\-consume() interceptors may be called from this function prior to passing message to application. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a53511739a2cf498b8d88287fef6873ce}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT ssize\_\-t rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch (rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkt}, \/  int32\_\-t {\em partition}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms}, \/  {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$$\ast$ {\em rkmessages}, \/  size\_\-t {\em rkmessages\_\-size})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a53511739a2cf498b8d88287fef6873ce}


Consume up to {\ttfamily rkmessages\_\-size} from topic {\ttfamily rkt} and {\ttfamily partition} putting a pointer to each message in the application provided array {\ttfamily rkmessages} (of size {\ttfamily rkmessages\_\-size} entries). `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch()` provides higher throughput performance than `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume()`.

{\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms} is the maximum amount of time to wait for all of {\ttfamily rkmessages\_\-size} messages to be put into {\ttfamily rkmessages}. If no messages were available within the timeout period this function returns 0 and {\ttfamily rkmessages} remains untouched. This differs somewhat from `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume()`.

The message objects must be destroyed with `rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-destroy()` when the application is done with it.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of rkmessages added in {\ttfamily rkmessages}, or -\/1 on error (same error codes as for `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume()`.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
on\_\-consume() interceptors may be called from this function prior to passing message to application. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a303fa0f0da7f3c28bed35570adc983c6}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT int rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback (rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkt}, \/  int32\_\-t {\em partition}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms}, \/  void($\ast$)({\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$rkmessage, void $\ast$opaque) {\em consume\_\-cb}, \/  void $\ast$ {\em opaque})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a303fa0f0da7f3c28bed35570adc983c6}


Consumes messages from topic {\ttfamily rkt} and {\ttfamily partition}, calling the provided callback for each consumed messsage. `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback()` provides higher throughput performance than both `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume()` and `rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch()`.

{\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms} is the maximum amount of time to wait for one or more messages to arrive.

The provided {\ttfamily consume\_\-cb} function is called for each message, the application {\bfseries MUST} {\bfseries NOT} call `rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-destroy()` on the provided {\ttfamily rkmessage}.

The {\ttfamily opaque} argument is passed to the 'consume\_\-cb' as {\ttfamily opaque}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of messages processed or -\/1 on error.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume()}
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
on\_\-consume() interceptors may be called from this function prior to passing message to application. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a8ff0b80fccb3a5bd31b1baaf20e4ca16}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-queue@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-queue}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-queue@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-queue}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-queue}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t}$\ast$ rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-queue (rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkqu}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a8ff0b80fccb3a5bd31b1baaf20e4ca16}


Consume from queue. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_aa49d14e8b742365f9f25d35318ff0b7e}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a3d949238471993b18537855aad28fa23}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch\_\-queue@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch\_\-queue}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch\_\-queue@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch\_\-queue}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch\_\-queue}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT ssize\_\-t rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch\_\-queue (rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkqu}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms}, \/  {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$$\ast$ {\em rkmessages}, \/  size\_\-t {\em rkmessages\_\-size})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a3d949238471993b18537855aad28fa23}


Consume batch of messages from queue. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a53511739a2cf498b8d88287fef6873ce}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-batch()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_abb1aaca2499c2e7d6da37dc28953d532}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback\_\-queue@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback\_\-queue}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback\_\-queue@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback\_\-queue}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback\_\-queue}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT int rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback\_\-queue (rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkqu}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms}, \/  void($\ast$)({\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$rkmessage, void $\ast$opaque) {\em consume\_\-cb}, \/  void $\ast$ {\em opaque})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_abb1aaca2499c2e7d6da37dc28953d532}


Consume multiple messages from queue with callback. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a303fa0f0da7f3c28bed35570adc983c6}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consume\_\-callback()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a784186db1d2cb6ceebcd5606d38db4c4}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-offset\_\-store@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-offset\_\-store}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-offset\_\-store@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-offset\_\-store}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-offset\_\-store}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-offset\_\-store (rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkt}, \/  int32\_\-t {\em partition}, \/  int64\_\-t {\em offset})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a784186db1d2cb6ceebcd5606d38db4c4}


Store offset {\ttfamily offset} for topic {\ttfamily rkt} partition {\ttfamily partition}. The offset will be committed (written) to the offset store according to {\ttfamily `auto}.commit.interval.ms` or manual offset-\/less commit()

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
{\ttfamily `enable}.auto.offset.store` must be set to \char`\"{}false\char`\"{} when using this API.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR on success or an error code on error. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a047b1e21236fba30898c7c563c2c6777}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-offsets\_\-store@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-offsets\_\-store}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-offsets\_\-store@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-offsets\_\-store}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-offsets\_\-store}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-offsets\_\-store (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em offsets})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a047b1e21236fba30898c7c563c2c6777}


Store offsets for next auto-\/commit for one or more partitions. The offset will be committed (written) to the offset store according to {\ttfamily `auto}.commit.interval.ms` or manual offset-\/less commit().

Per-\/partition success/error status propagated through each partition's {\ttfamily }.err field.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
{\ttfamily `enable}.auto.offset.store` must be set to \char`\"{}false\char`\"{} when using this API.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR on success, or RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-UNKNOWN\_\-PARTITION if none of the offsets could be stored, or RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-INVALID\_\-ARG if {\ttfamily enable.auto.offset.store} is true. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a0ebe15e9d0f39ccc84e9686f0fcf46f1}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-subscribe@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-subscribe}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-subscribe@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-subscribe}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-subscribe}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-subscribe (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  const {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em topics})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a0ebe15e9d0f39ccc84e9686f0fcf46f1}


Subscribe to topic set using balanced consumer groups. Wildcard (regex) topics are supported by the librdkafka assignor: any topic name in the {\ttfamily topics} list that is prefixed with {\ttfamily $\backslash$\char`\"{}$^\wedge$$\backslash$\char`\"{}} will be regex-\/matched to the full list of topics in the cluster and matching topics will be added to the subscription list.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR on success or RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-INVALID\_\-ARG if list is empty, contains invalid topics or regexes. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ab66a2c014db2e652aa12466b137a6200}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-subscription@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-subscription}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-subscription@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-subscription}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-subscription}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-subscription (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$$\ast$ {\em topics})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ab66a2c014db2e652aa12466b137a6200}


Returns the current topic subscription. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An error code on failure, otherwise {\ttfamily topic} is updated to point to a newly allocated topic list (possibly empty).
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The application is responsible for calling rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-destroy on the returned list. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a65cc6cb9bd72c4084f074af0361ceddf}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-poll@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-poll}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-poll@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-poll}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-poll}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t}$\ast$ rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-poll (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a65cc6cb9bd72c4084f074af0361ceddf}


Poll the consumer for messages or events. Will block for at most {\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms} milliseconds.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
An application should make sure to call consumer\_\-poll() at regular intervals, even if no messages are expected, to serve any queued callbacks waiting to be called. This is especially important when a rebalance\_\-cb has been registered as it needs to be called and handled properly to synchronize internal consumer state.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A message object which is a proper message if {\ttfamily -\/$>$err} is RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR, or an event or error for any other value.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
on\_\-consume() interceptors may be called from this function prior to passing message to application.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{structrd__kafka__message__t}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a37b54d329e12d745889defe96e7d043d}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-close@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-close}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-close@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-close}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-close}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-close (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a37b54d329e12d745889defe96e7d043d}


Close down the KafkaConsumer. \begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This call will block until the consumer has revoked its assignment, calling the {\ttfamily rebalance\_\-cb} if it is configured, committed offsets to broker, and left the consumer group. The maximum blocking time is roughly limited to session.timeout.ms.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An error code indicating if the consumer close was succesful or not.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The application still needs to call \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ac052e92621dcaa3a336dbf826e0d7794}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-destroy()} after this call finishes to clean up the underlying handle resources. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a0566419eff2001f8371e3b50aa7d26e9}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-assign@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-assign}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-assign@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-assign}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-assign}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-assign (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  const {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em partitions})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a0566419eff2001f8371e3b50aa7d26e9}


Atomic assignment of partitions to consume. The new {\ttfamily partitions} will replace the existing assignment.

When used from a rebalance callback the application shall pass the partition list passed to the callback (or a copy of it) (even if the list is empty) rather than NULL to maintain internal join state.

A zero-\/length {\ttfamily partitions} will treat the partitions as a valid, albeit empty, assignment, and maintain internal state, while a {\ttfamily NULL} value for {\ttfamily partitions} will reset and clear the internal state. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a10a00cc624a46209fe1192cfc56cce59}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-assignment@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-assignment}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-assignment@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-assignment}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-assignment}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-assignment (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$$\ast$ {\em partitions})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a10a00cc624a46209fe1192cfc56cce59}


Returns the current partition assignment. \begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
An error code on failure, otherwise {\ttfamily partitions} is updated to point to a newly allocated partition list (possibly empty).
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
The application is responsible for calling rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-destroy on the returned list. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ab96539928328f14c3c9177ea0c896c87}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  const {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em offsets}, \/  int {\em async})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ab96539928328f14c3c9177ea0c896c87}


Commit offsets on broker for the provided list of partitions. {\ttfamily offsets} should contain {\ttfamily topic}, {\ttfamily partition}, {\ttfamily offset} and possibly {\ttfamily metadata}. If {\ttfamily offsets} is NULL the current partition assignment will be used instead.

If {\ttfamily async} is false this operation will block until the broker offset commit is done, returning the resulting success or error code.

If a \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a1ab8bb9e8d8cdd5906f9e060b506f2eb}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-offset\_\-commit\_\-cb()} offset commit callback has been configured the callback will be enqueued for a future call to \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll()}, \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a65cc6cb9bd72c4084f074af0361ceddf}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-poll()} or similar. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a99fb25d50216e4e20d303bf8a4a62883}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit\_\-message@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit\_\-message}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit\_\-message@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit\_\-message}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit\_\-message}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit\_\-message (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  const {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em rkmessage}, \/  int {\em async})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a99fb25d50216e4e20d303bf8a4a62883}


Commit message's offset on broker for the message's partition. \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ab96539928328f14c3c9177ea0c896c87}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_aa793dd9c195f39bcb69465cebf534c47}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit\_\-queue@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit\_\-queue}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit\_\-queue@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit\_\-queue}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit\_\-queue}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit\_\-queue (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  const {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em offsets}, \/  rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkqu}, \/  void($\ast$)(rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} err, {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$offsets, void $\ast$opaque) {\em cb}, \/  void $\ast$ {\em opaque})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_aa793dd9c195f39bcb69465cebf534c47}


Commit offsets on broker for the provided list of partitions. See rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit for {\ttfamily offsets} semantics.

The result of the offset commit will be posted on the provided {\ttfamily rkqu} queue.

If the application uses one of the poll APIs (\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll()}, \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a65cc6cb9bd72c4084f074af0361ceddf}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-consumer\_\-poll()}, \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a2f147ed1c554c9048893fb1adde86dfa}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-queue\_\-poll()}, ..) to serve the queue the {\ttfamily cb} callback is required. {\ttfamily opaque} is passed to the callback.

If using the event API the callback is ignored and the offset commit result will be returned as an RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-EVENT\_\-COMMIT event. The {\ttfamily opaque} value will be available with \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8650ed2a19108d490a65c9aff3e66525}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-event\_\-opaque()}

If {\ttfamily rkqu} is NULL a temporary queue will be created and the callback will be served by this call.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ab96539928328f14c3c9177ea0c896c87}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-commit()} 

\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a1ab8bb9e8d8cdd5906f9e060b506f2eb}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-offset\_\-commit\_\-cb()} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a39846ae321a03c4679c9c659f18adf13}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-committed@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-committed}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-committed@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-committed}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-committed}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-committed (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em partitions}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a39846ae321a03c4679c9c659f18adf13}


Retrieve committed offsets for topics+partitions. The {\ttfamily offset} field of each requested partition will either be set to stored offset or to RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-OFFSET\_\-INVALID in case there was no stored offset for that partition.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR on success in which case the {\ttfamily offset} or {\ttfamily err} field of each {\ttfamily partitions'} element is filled in with the stored offset, or a partition specific error. Else returns an error code. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a6e9e36bd9e6bf84a9f3092fcbfa3a9ac}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-position@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-position}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-position@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-position}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-position}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-position (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-partition\_\-list\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em partitions})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a6e9e36bd9e6bf84a9f3092fcbfa3a9ac}


Retrieve current positions (offsets) for topics+partitions. The {\ttfamily offset} field of each requested partition will be set to the offset of the last consumed message + 1, or RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-OFFSET\_\-INVALID in case there was no previous message.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR on success in which case the {\ttfamily offset} or {\ttfamily err} field of each {\ttfamily partitions'} element is filled in with the stored offset, or a partition specific error. Else returns an error code. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ae24d8ebf1ea15ed8ea0ea40f74662736}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT int rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce (rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkt}, \/  int32\_\-t {\em partition}, \/  int {\em msgflags}, \/  void $\ast$ {\em payload}, \/  size\_\-t {\em len}, \/  const void $\ast$ {\em key}, \/  size\_\-t {\em keylen}, \/  void $\ast$ {\em msg\_\-opaque})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ae24d8ebf1ea15ed8ea0ea40f74662736}


Produce and send a single message to broker. {\ttfamily rkt} is the target topic which must have been previously created with `rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-new()`.

`rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce()` is an asynch non-\/blocking API.

{\ttfamily partition} is the target partition, either:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-PARTITION\_\-UA (unassigned) for automatic partitioning using the topic's partitioner function, or
\item a fixed partition (0..N)
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\ttfamily msgflags} is zero or more of the following flags OR:ed together: RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-MSG\_\-F\_\-BLOCK -\/ block {\ttfamily produce$\ast$}() call if {\ttfamily queue.buffering.max.messages} or {\ttfamily queue.buffering.max.kbytes} are exceeded. Messages are considered in-\/queue from the point they are accepted by produce() until their corresponding delivery report callback/event returns. It is thus a requirement to call \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll()} (or equiv.) from a separate thread when F\_\-BLOCK is used. See WARNING on {\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-MSG\_\-F\_\-BLOCK} above.

RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-MSG\_\-F\_\-FREE -\/ rdkafka will free(3) {\ttfamily payload} when it is done with it. RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-MSG\_\-F\_\-COPY -\/ the {\ttfamily payload} data will be copied and the {\ttfamily payload} pointer will not be used by rdkafka after the call returns. RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-MSG\_\-F\_\-PARTITION -\/ produce\_\-batch() will honour per-\/message partition, either set manually or by the configured partitioner.

..\_\-F\_\-FREE and ..\_\-F\_\-COPY are mutually exclusive.

If the function returns -\/1 and RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-MSG\_\-F\_\-FREE was specified, then the memory associated with the payload is still the caller's responsibility.

{\ttfamily payload} is the message payload of size {\ttfamily len} bytes.

{\ttfamily key} is an optional message key of size {\ttfamily keylen} bytes, if non-\/NULL it will be passed to the topic partitioner as well as be sent with the message to the broker and passed on to the consumer.

{\ttfamily msg\_\-opaque} is an optional application-\/provided per-\/message opaque pointer that will provided in the delivery report callback (`dr\_\-cb`) for referencing this message.

\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
on\_\-send() and on\_\-acknowledgement() interceptors may be called from this function. on\_\-acknowledgement() will only be called if the message fails partitioning.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
0 on success or -\/1 on error in which case errno is set accordingly:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item ENOBUFS -\/ maximum number of outstanding messages has been reached: \char`\"{}queue.buffering.max.messages\char`\"{} (RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-QUEUE\_\-FULL)
\item EMSGSIZE -\/ message is larger than configured max size: \char`\"{}messages.max.bytes\char`\"{}. (RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-MSG\_\-SIZE\_\-TOO\_\-LARGE)
\item ESRCH -\/ requested {\ttfamily partition} is unknown in the Kafka cluster. (RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-UNKNOWN\_\-PARTITION)
\item ENOENT -\/ topic is unknown in the Kafka cluster. (RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-UNKNOWN\_\-TOPIC)
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_abeabf8589c657d7a3ec5a1411a7de91d}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-errno2err()} to convert `errno` to rdkafka error code. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ac3a111ec3e6729609d498fec7b619efc}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-producev@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-producev}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-producev@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-producev}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-producev}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-producev (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/   {\em ...})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ac3a111ec3e6729609d498fec7b619efc}


Produce and send a single message to broker. The message is defined by a va-\/arg list using {\ttfamily rd\_\-kafka\_\-vtype\_\-t} tag tuples which must be terminated with a single {\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-V\_\-END}.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR} on success, else an error code. {\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-CONFLICT} is returned if \_\-V\_\-HEADER and \_\-V\_\-HEADERS are mixed.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ae24d8ebf1ea15ed8ea0ea40f74662736}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce}, \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a03c74ceba678b4e7a624310160a02165}{RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-V\_\-END} 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a7ad15c71f228c47946500a0e5c6f88ed}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce\_\-batch@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce\_\-batch}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce\_\-batch@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce\_\-batch}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce\_\-batch}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT int rd\_\-kafka\_\-produce\_\-batch (rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rkt}, \/  int32\_\-t {\em partition}, \/  int {\em msgflags}, \/  {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-message\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em rkmessages}, \/  int {\em message\_\-cnt})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a7ad15c71f228c47946500a0e5c6f88ed}


Produce multiple messages. If partition is RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-PARTITION\_\-UA the configured partitioner will be run for each message (slower), otherwise the messages will be enqueued to the specified partition directly (faster).

The messages are provided in the array {\ttfamily rkmessages} of count {\ttfamily message\_\-cnt} elements. The {\ttfamily partition} and {\ttfamily msgflags} are used for all provided messages.

Honoured {\ttfamily rkmessages}\mbox{[}\mbox{]} fields are:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item payload,len Message payload and length
\item key,key\_\-len Optional message key
\item \_\-private Message opaque pointer (msg\_\-opaque)
\item err Will be set according to success or failure. Application only needs to check for errors if return value != {\ttfamily message\_\-cnt}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of messages succesfully enqueued for producing.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This interface does NOT support setting message headers on the provided {\ttfamily rkmessages}. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_aaff06c4372bce917c17f3c1a5d8b205d}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-flush@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-flush}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-flush@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-flush}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-flush}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-flush (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_aaff06c4372bce917c17f3c1a5d8b205d}


Wait until all outstanding produce requests, et.al, are completed. This should typically be done prior to destroying a producer instance to make sure all queued and in-\/flight produce requests are completed before terminating. \begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
This function will call \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ad50c431e3a29d14da534db49bd0682a4}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-poll()} and thus trigger callbacks.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-TIMED\_\-OUT if {\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms} was reached before all outstanding requests were completed, else RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a84bba4a4b13fdb515f1a22d6fd4f7344}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-metadata@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-metadata}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-metadata@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-metadata}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-metadata}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-metadata (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  int {\em all\_\-topics}, \/  rd\_\-kafka\_\-topic\_\-t $\ast$ {\em only\_\-rkt}, \/  const struct rd\_\-kafka\_\-metadata $\ast$$\ast$ {\em metadatap}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a84bba4a4b13fdb515f1a22d6fd4f7344}


Request Metadata from broker. Parameters:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily all\_\-topics} if non-\/zero: request info about all topics in cluster, if zero: only request info about locally known topics.
\item {\ttfamily only\_\-rkt} only request info about this topic
\item {\ttfamily metadatap} pointer to hold metadata result. The {\ttfamily $\ast$metadatap} pointer must be released with \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a0b4ee98ab1c76f3504edf9eed986844e}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-metadata\_\-destroy()}.
\item {\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms} maximum response time before failing.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Returns RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR on success (in which case $\ast$metadatap) will be set, else RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-TIMED\_\-OUT on timeout or other error code on error. \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a6cfc79819453ecd4aa94fbae6dbbea0a}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-list\_\-groups@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-list\_\-groups}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-list\_\-groups@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-list\_\-groups}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-list\_\-groups}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-list\_\-groups (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  const char $\ast$ {\em group}, \/  const struct {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-group\_\-list} $\ast$$\ast$ {\em grplistp}, \/  int {\em timeout\_\-ms})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a6cfc79819453ecd4aa94fbae6dbbea0a}


List and describe client groups in cluster. {\ttfamily group} is an optional group name to describe, otherwise ({\ttfamily NULL}) all groups are returned.

{\ttfamily timeout\_\-ms} is the (approximate) maximum time to wait for response from brokers and must be a positive value.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
{\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-NO\_\-ERROR} on success and {\ttfamily grplistp} is updated to point to a newly allocated list of groups. {\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-PARTIAL} if not all brokers responded in time but at least one group is returned in {\ttfamily grplistlp}. {\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-TIMED\_\-OUT} if no groups were returned in the given timeframe but not all brokers have yet responded, or if the list of brokers in the cluster could not be obtained within the given timeframe. {\ttfamily RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-TRANSPORT} if no brokers were found. Other error codes may also be returned from the request layer.
\end{DoxyReturn}
The {\ttfamily grplistp} remains untouched if any error code is returned, with the exception of RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-PARTIAL which behaves as RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-NO\_\-ERROR (success) but with an incomplete group list.

\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_ab28e1cb749e7e62168107ccdee1960ea}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-group\_\-list\_\-destroy()} to release list memory. 
\end{DoxySeeAlso}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ab83da8da989fe41693d78d982c7ae6b7}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-brokers\_\-add@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-brokers\_\-add}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-brokers\_\-add@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-brokers\_\-add}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-brokers\_\-add}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT int rd\_\-kafka\_\-brokers\_\-add (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  const char $\ast$ {\em brokerlist})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ab83da8da989fe41693d78d982c7ae6b7}


Adds one or more brokers to the kafka handle's list of initial bootstrap brokers. Additional brokers will be discovered automatically as soon as rdkafka connects to a broker by querying the broker metadata.

If a broker name resolves to multiple addresses (and possibly address families) all will be used for connection attempts in round-\/robin fashion.

{\ttfamily brokerlist} is a ,-\/separated list of brokers in the format: {\ttfamily $<$broker1$>$},$<$broker2$>$,.. Where each broker is in either the host or URL based format: {\ttfamily $<$host$>$}\mbox{[}:$<$port$>$\mbox{]} {\ttfamily $<$proto$>$}://$<$host$>$\mbox{[}:port\mbox{]} {\ttfamily $<$proto$>$} is either {\ttfamily PLAINTEXT}, {\ttfamily SSL}, {\ttfamily SASL}, {\ttfamily SASL\_\-PLAINTEXT} The two formats can be mixed but ultimately the value of the `security.protocol` config property decides what brokers are allowed.

Example: brokerlist = \char`\"{}broker1:10000,broker2\char`\"{} brokerlist = \char`\"{}SSL://broker3:9000,ssl://broker2\char`\"{}

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
the number of brokers successfully added.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Brokers may also be defined with the {\ttfamily metadata.broker.list} or {\ttfamily bootstrap.servers} configuration property (preferred method). 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_a9e4af9adee414af74c7817403f7c4a53}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-logger@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-logger}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-logger@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-logger}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-logger}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT RD\_\-DEPRECATED void rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-logger (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  void($\ast$)(const rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$rk, int level, const char $\ast$fac, const char $\ast$buf) {\em func})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a9e4af9adee414af74c7817403f7c4a53}


Set logger function. The default is to print to stderr, but a syslog logger is also available, see rd\_\-kafka\_\-log\_\-(print$|$syslog) for the builtin alternatives. Alternatively the application may provide its own logger callback. Or pass 'func' as NULL to disable logging.

\begin{Desc}
\item[\hyperlink{deprecated__deprecated000005}{Deprecated}]Use \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a06ade2ca41f32eb82c6f7e3d4acbe19f}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-set\_\-log\_\-cb()}\end{Desc}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
{\ttfamily rk} may be passed as NULL in the callback. 
\end{DoxyRemark}
\hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_acadeefced6bb60acd27e7a0dad553aa4}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-log\_\-level@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-log\_\-level}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-log\_\-level@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-log\_\-level}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-log\_\-level}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT void rd\_\-kafka\_\-set\_\-log\_\-level (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk}, \/  int {\em level})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_acadeefced6bb60acd27e7a0dad553aa4}


Specifies the maximum logging level produced by internal kafka logging and debugging. If the {\ttfamily $\backslash$\char`\"{}debug$\backslash$\char`\"{}} configuration property is set the level is automatically adjusted to {\ttfamily LOG\_\-DEBUG} (7). \hypertarget{rdkafka_8h_ad4b3b7659cf9a79d3353810d6b625bb7}{
\index{rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}!rd\_\-kafka\_\-outq\_\-len@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-outq\_\-len}}
\index{rd\_\-kafka\_\-outq\_\-len@{rd\_\-kafka\_\-outq\_\-len}!rdkafka.h@{rdkafka.h}}
\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-outq\_\-len}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT int rd\_\-kafka\_\-outq\_\-len (rd\_\-kafka\_\-t $\ast$ {\em rk})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_ad4b3b7659cf9a79d3353810d6b625bb7}


Returns the current out queue length. The out queue contains messages waiting to be sent to, or acknowledged by, the broker.

An application should wait for this queue to reach zero before terminating to make sure outstanding requests (such as offset commits) are fully processed.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
number of messages in the out queue. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\label{rdkafka_8h_ad76a1b2d6c4f1727725b075678b88793}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}

\end{DoxyReturn}

the number of events served.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}

\end{DoxyRemark}

\subsubsection[{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-interceptor\_\-add\_\-on\_\-new}]{\setlength{\rightskip}{0pt plus 5cm}RD\_\-EXPORT {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-resp\_\-err\_\-t} rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-interceptor\_\-add\_\-on\_\-new (rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-t $\ast$ {\em conf}, \/  const char $\ast$ {\em ic\_\-name}, \/  {\bf rd\_\-kafka\_\-interceptor\_\-f\_\-on\_\-new\_\-t} $\ast$ {\em on\_\-new}, \/  void $\ast$ {\em ic\_\-opaque})}}
\label{rdkafka_8h_a002ef1d350176725b6e9ba93548edf40}


Append an on\_\-new() interceptor. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em conf}]Configuration object. \item[{\em ic\_\-name}]Interceptor name, used in logging. \item[{\em on\_\-send}]Function pointer. \item[{\em ic\_\-opaque}]Opaque value that will be passed to the function.\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyRemark}{Remarks}
Since the on\_\-new() interceptor is added to the configuration object it may be copied by \hyperlink{rdkafka_8h_a8cbfe15c6978ff09870e82cb524c673d}{rd\_\-kafka\_\-conf\_\-dup()}. An interceptor implementation must thus be able to handle the same interceptor,ic\_\-opaque tuple to be used by multiple client instances.

An interceptor plugin should check the return value to make sure it has not already been added.
\end{DoxyRemark}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR on success or RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-CONFLICT if an existing intercepted with the same {\ttfamily ic\_\-name} and function has already been added to {\ttfamily conf}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Append an on\_\-commit() interceptor. 
\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
\item[{\em rk}]Client instance. \item[{\em ic\_\-name}]Interceptor name, used in logging. \item[{\em on\_\-commit()}]Function pointer. \item[{\em ic\_\-opaque}]Opaque value that will be passed to the function.\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-NO\_\-ERROR on success or RD\_\-KAFKA\_\-RESP\_\-ERR\_\-\_\-CONFLICT if an existing intercepted with the same {\ttfamily ic\_\-name} and function has already been added to {\ttfamily conf}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
